@ $mol_mem
page_list(next?: number[]) { return next ?? [] } // –Ω–æ–º–µ—Ä–∞ —Å—Ñ–µ—Ç—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü

@ $mol_mem_key
page_data(page: number) {
    return this.$.$mol_fetch.json( `url?page=${page}` ) // –∫–µ—à–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç —Å—Ñ–µ—Ç—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ
}

@ $mol_action
pages_load() {
  let total = Infinity
  let page = 1
  do {
      const res = this.page_data(page)
      total = res.totalPages
      page += 1
      this.page_list( [...this.page_list(), page ) ]
  } while(total - page > 0)
}

–∏–ª–∏ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å—Ñ–µ—Ç—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –º–∞—Å—Å–∏–≤–µ –≤ $mol_mem —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å –∞ –Ω–µ –≤ $mol_mem_key

@ $mol_mem
data() {
  let total = Infinity
  let page = 1
  const pages = []
  do {
      const res = this.$.$mol_fetch.json(`url?page=${page}`)
      total = res.totalPages
      page += 1
      pages.push(res)
  } while(total - page > 0)

  return pages
}

async getDateFromTimeStamp(timestamp) {
    const date = new Date(parseInt(timestamp, 10));
    return `${date.getMonth() + 1 < 10 ? `0${date.getMonth() + 1}` : date.getMonth() + 1
      }/${date.getDate() < 10 ? `0${date.getDate()}` : date.getDate()
      }/${date.getFullYear()}`;
  }


async getDateFromTimeStamp(timestamp) {
    const date = new Date(parseInt(timestamp, 10));

    const month = date.getMonth() + 1 < 10 ? `0${date.getMonth() + 1}` : date.getMonth() + 1;
    const days = date.getDate() < 10 ? `0${date.getDate()}` : date.getDate();
    const year = date.getFullYear();
    return `${days}/${month}/${year}`;
  }

@ $mol_wire_field inProgress = false
@ $mol_wire_field articleSlug = undefined

@ $mol_wire_field title = ''
@ $mol_wire_field description = ''
@ $mol_wire_field body = ''
@ $mol_wire_field tagList = []

@ $mol_action loadInitialData() {
  if (!this.aricleSlug) return
  this.inProgress = true

  try {
    const article = articlesStore.loadArticle(this.articleSlug())
    this.title = article.title
    this.description = article.description
    this.body = article.body
    this.tagList = article.tagList
  } finally {
    this.inProgress = false
  }
}

slug(next?: string) {
   return next ?? ''

@ $mol_mem
article() {
  return $mol_fetch.json(`/article/${this.slug()}`)
}

@ $mol_mem
article_title(next?: string) {
  return next ?? this.article()?.title ?? ''

article_description(next?: string) {
  return next ?? this.article()?.description ?? ''

}

  @observable inProgress = false;
  @observable articleSlug = undefined;
  
  @observable title = '';
  @observable description = '';
  @observable body = '';
  @observable tagList = [];
  
  @action loadInitialData() {
    if (!this.articleSlug) return Promise.resolve();
    this.inProgress = true;
    return articlesStore.loadArticle(this.articleSlug, { acceptCached: true })
      .then(action((article) => {
        if (!article) throw new Error('Can\'t load original article');
        this.title = article.title;
        this.description = article.description;
        this.body = article.body;
        this.tagList = article.tagList;
      }))
      .finally(action(() => { this.inProgress = false; }));
  }

    const message = reason instanceof Error ? reason.stack : reason;

    const message = error instanceof Error ? error.stack : error;

    process.exit(1);
